    Click on any release to be taken to the corresponding release on the Releases page.

    Key to symbols:

    • † after an issue number denotes the lack of an official catalogue number.
    • * after release denotes that only part of the take has been used for the issued title
    • ‡ indicates a release is not confirmed.
    • # is added to a title to distinguish it from a different tune of the same name
    • * after a New DESOR number indicates it is not from the New DESOR or a correction sheet, but has been unofficially assigned elsewhere
    • External links have the following codes
      • (D): Discogs.com
      • (MB): MusicBrainz.org
      • (A): Amazon (US)
      • (AM): AllMusic
      • (AR): Archive.org
      • (F): Misc file
      • (S): Spotify
      • (T): Tidal
      • (YT): YouTube
